Local Roadway Facilities




                           1
                                         Local Roadway Facilities

American Canyon Road
American Canyon Road is an east-west, major arterial street that connects to Interstate 80 to the east
and SR-29 to the west. The arterial is two lanes wide between Interstate 80 and Newell Drive and four
lanes wide with a landscaped median between Newell Drive and Wetlands Edge Road, its western
terminus. A bicycle lane is provided in each direction between SR-29 and Wetlands Edge Road. The
posted speed limit on the street is 40 to 45 mph in the immediate vicinity of the project.

Silver Oak Trail
Silver Oak Trail is a north-south collector street that connects residential areas in the city of American
Canyon to American Canyon Road. The road is two lanes wide and extends from American Canyon Road
to the south to Newell Drive to the north. Sidewalks are provided in both directions. The posted speed
limit on the street is 25 mph.

Newell Drive
Newell Drive is a north-south collector street that connects residential areas in American Canyon to
American Canyon Road. The road is two to four lanes wide and extends from American Canyon Road to
the south to Donaldson Way to the north. A sidewalk is provided on the western side of the street. The
posted speed limit on the street is 35 mph.

Donaldson Way
Donaldson Way is an east-west collector street that connects residential areas in American Canyon to SR-
29. The road is two lanes wide and extends from Newell Drive to the east to SR-29 to Eucalyptus Drive to
the west. Sidewalks are provided in both directions in most places between SR-29 and Newell Drive. The
posted speed limit on the street is 25 mph.

South Napa Junction Road
South Napa Junction Road is a short east-west local street that connects primarily industrial land uses to
SR-29. The road is two lanes wide and extends from the train tracks that parallel SR-29 to the east to
Melvin Road to the west. The posted speed limit on the street is 25 mph.

Poco Way
Poco Way is an east-west local street that connects residential areas in American Canyon to SR-29. The
road is two lanes wide and extends from SR-29 in the east to Melvin Road to the west. Sidewalks or
curbs are provided on the south side of the street but not on the north side of the street. The posted
speed limit on the street is 25 mph.

Rio Del Mar
Rio Del Mar is an east-west collector street that connects residential areas in American Canyon to SR-29.
The road is two lanes wide and extends from SR-29 in the east to Wetlands Edge Road to the west.
Sidewalks are provided in both directions. The posted speed limit on the street is 25 mph.




                                                                                                             2
Eucalyptus Drive
Eucalyptus Drive is an east-west local street that connects commercial and residential areas in American
Canyon to SR-29. The road is two to four lanes wide and extends from Napa Junction Road to Wetlands
Edge Road, with a discontinuous connection across SR-29. Sidewalks are provided in both directions east
of SR-29. The posted speed limit on the street is 25 mph.

Napa Junction Road
Napa Junction Road is a short east-west collector street that connects primarily industrial areas to SR-29.
The road is two lanes wide and extends from Eucalyptus Drive to Hess Road. The posted speed limit on
the street is 25 mph.

Green Island Road
Green Island Road is an east-west collector street that connects industrial and commercial areas south of
the Napa County Airport to the southbound lanes of SR-29. The road is two lanes wide and extends from
SR-29 and terminates southwest of the airport. The posted speed limit on the street is 40 mph.

Paoli Loop Road
Paoli Loop Road is a short east-west local street that connects industrial and commercial areas to the
northbound lanes of SR-29. The road is two lanes wide and extends from Green Island Road to SR-29
northbound.

North-South Kelly Road
North-South Kelly Road is a north-south collector street that connects primarily industrial areas to SR-29
and SR-12. The road is two lanes wide and extends from SR-12/29 to Devlin Road. The posted speed
limit on the street is 50 mph east of SR-29.

Airport Boulevard
Airport Boulevard is an east-west arterial street that connects commercial areas near the Napa County
Airport to SR-29. The road is four lanes wide with a landscaped median, extending from SR-29 to the
Napa County Airport. The posted speed limit on the street is 45 mph.

Devlin Road
Devlin Road is a north-south collector street that provides access to commercial and industrial areas
near the Napa County Airport. The road is two to four lanes wide, extending from Soscol Ferry Road to
South Kelly Road, providing the primary local access to the Project site. The posted speed limit on the
street is 45 mph.

Airpark Road
Airpark Road is a short north-south local street that provides access to commercial areas near the Napa
County Airport. The road is two lanes wide and extends from Technology Way to Devlin Road.

Kirkland Ranch Road
Kirkland Ranch Road is a short east-west local street that connects rural farm areas to SR-12. The road is
two lanes wide.




                                                                                                             3
Tower Road
Tower Road is a short east-west local street that connects industrial areas near the Napa County Airport
to SR-29. The road is two lanes wide and extends west from SR-29, terminating west of Devlin Road. The
posted speed limit on the street is 25 mph.

Meadows Drive
Meadows Drive is an east-west collector street that connects residential areas in Vallejo to SR-29. The
road is four lanes wide and extends from SR-29 to Catalina Way. The posted speed limit on the street is
35 mph.

Mini Drive
Mini Drive is an east-west collector street that connects residential areas in Vallejo to SR-29. The road is
two lanes wide between Lewis Brown Drive and SR-29 and four lanes wide between SR-29 and Dutch
Flat Road. Sidewalks are provided in both directions. The posted speed limit on the street is 30 mph.
